4225:       PetscCallHIPSPARSE(hipsparseCreateCsr(&Cmat->matDescr, Ccsr->num_rows, Ccsr->num_cols, Ccsr->num_entries, Ccsr->row_offsets->data().get(), Ccsr->column_indices->data().get(), Ccsr->values->data().get(), HIPSPARSE_INDEX_32I, HIPSPARSE_INDEX_32I, HIPSPARSE_INDEX_BASE_ZERO, hipsparse_scalartype));

4227:       if (A->form_explicit_transpose && B->form_explicit_transpose) { /* if A and B have the transpose, generate C transpose too */
4228:         PetscCall(MatSeqAIJHIPSPARSEFormExplicitTranspose(A));
4229:         PetscCall(MatSeqAIJHIPSPARSEFormExplicitTranspose(B));
4230:         PetscBool                      AT = Acusp->matTranspose ? PETSC_TRUE : PETSC_FALSE, BT = Bcusp->matTranspose ? PETSC_TRUE : PETSC_FALSE;
4231:         Mat_SeqAIJHIPSPARSEMultStruct *CmatT = new Mat_SeqAIJHIPSPARSEMultStruct;
4232:         CsrMatrix                     *CcsrT = new CsrMatrix;
4233:         CsrMatrix                     *AcsrT = AT ? (CsrMatrix *)Acusp->matTranspose->mat : NULL;
4234:         CsrMatrix                     *BcsrT = BT ? (CsrMatrix *)Bcusp->matTranspose->mat : NULL;

4236:         (*C)->form_explicit_transpose = PETSC_TRUE;
4237:         (*C)->transupdated            = PETSC_TRUE;
4238:         Ccusp->rowoffsets_gpu         = NULL;
4239:         CmatT->cprowIndices           = NULL;
4240:         CmatT->mat                    = CcsrT;
4241:         CcsrT->num_rows               = n;
4242:         CcsrT->num_cols               = m;
4243:         CcsrT->num_entries            = c->nz;
4244:         CcsrT->row_offsets            = new THRUSTINTARRAY32(n + 1);
4245:         CcsrT->column_indices         = new THRUSTINTARRAY32(c->nz);
4246:         CcsrT->values                 = new THRUSTARRAY(c->nz);

4248:         PetscCall(PetscLogGpuTimeBegin());
4249:         auto rT = CcsrT->row_offsets->begin();
4250:         if (AT) {
4251:           rT = thrust::copy(AcsrT->row_offsets->begin(), AcsrT->row_offsets->end(), rT);
4252:           thrust::advance(rT, -1);
4253:         }
4254:         if (BT) {
4255:           auto titb = thrust::make_transform_iterator(BcsrT->row_offsets->begin(), Shift(a->nz));
4256:           auto tite = thrust::make_transform_iterator(BcsrT->row_offsets->end(), Shift(a->nz));
4257:           thrust::copy(titb, tite, rT);
4258:         }
4259:         auto cT = CcsrT->column_indices->begin();
4260:         if (AT) cT = thrust::copy(AcsrT->column_indices->begin(), AcsrT->column_indices->end(), cT);
4261:         if (BT) thrust::copy(BcsrT->column_indices->begin(), BcsrT->column_indices->end(), cT);
4262:         auto vT = CcsrT->values->begin();
4263:         if (AT) vT = thrust::copy(AcsrT->values->begin(), AcsrT->values->end(), vT);
4264:         if (BT) thrust::copy(BcsrT->values->begin(), BcsrT->values->end(), vT);
4265:         PetscCall(PetscLogGpuTimeEnd());

4267:         PetscCallHIPSPARSE(hipsparseCreateMatDescr(&CmatT->descr));
4268:         PetscCallHIPSPARSE(hipsparseSetMatIndexBase(CmatT->descr, HIPSPARSE_INDEX_BASE_ZERO));
4269:         PetscCallHIPSPARSE(hipsparseSetMatType(CmatT->descr, HIPSPARSE_MATRIX_TYPE_GENERAL));
4270:         PetscCallHIP(hipMalloc((void **)&(CmatT->alpha_one), sizeof(PetscScalar)));
4271:         PetscCallHIP(hipMalloc((void **)&(CmatT->beta_zero), sizeof(PetscScalar)));
4272:         PetscCallHIP(hipMalloc((void **)&(CmatT->beta_one), sizeof(PetscScalar)));
4273:         PetscCallHIP(hipMemcpy(CmatT->alpha_one, &PETSC_HIPSPARSE_ONE, sizeof(PetscScalar), hipMemcpyHostToDevice));
4274:         PetscCallHIP(hipMemcpy(CmatT->beta_zero, &PETSC_HIPSPARSE_ZERO, sizeof(PetscScalar), hipMemcpyHostToDevice));
4275:         PetscCallHIP(hipMemcpy(CmatT->beta_one, &PETSC_HIPSPARSE_ONE, sizeof(PetscScalar), hipMemcpyHostToDevice));

4277:         PetscCallHIPSPARSE(hipsparseCreateCsr(&CmatT->matDescr, CcsrT->num_rows, CcsrT->num_cols, CcsrT->num_entries, CcsrT->row_offsets->data().get(), CcsrT->column_indices->data().get(), CcsrT->values->data().get(), HIPSPARSE_INDEX_32I, HIPSPARSE_INDEX_32I, HIPSPARSE_INDEX_BASE_ZERO, hipsparse_scalartype));
4278:         Ccusp->matTranspose = CmatT;
4279:       }
4280:     }

4282:     c->singlemalloc = PETSC_FALSE;
4283:     c->free_a       = PETSC_TRUE;
4284:     c->free_ij      = PETSC_TRUE;
4285:     PetscCall(PetscMalloc1(m + 1, &c->i));
4286:     PetscCall(PetscMalloc1(c->nz, &c->j));
4287:     if (PetscDefined(USE_64BIT_INDICES)) { /* 32 to 64-bit conversion on the GPU and then copy to host (lazy) */
4288:       THRUSTINTARRAY ii(Ccsr->row_offsets->size());
4289:       THRUSTINTARRAY jj(Ccsr->column_indices->size());
4290:       ii = *Ccsr->row_offsets;
4291:       jj = *Ccsr->column_indices;
4292:       PetscCallHIP(hipMemcpy(c->i, ii.data().get(), Ccsr->row_offsets->size() * sizeof(PetscInt), hipMemcpyDeviceToHost));
4293:       PetscCallHIP(hipMemcpy(c->j, jj.data().get(), Ccsr->column_indices->size() * sizeof(PetscInt), hipMemcpyDeviceToHost));
4294:     } else {
4295:       PetscCallHIP(hipMemcpy(c->i, Ccsr->row_offsets->data().get(), Ccsr->row_offsets->size() * sizeof(PetscInt), hipMemcpyDeviceToHost));
4296:       PetscCallHIP(hipMemcpy(c->j, Ccsr->column_indices->data().get(), Ccsr->column_indices->size() * sizeof(PetscInt), hipMemcpyDeviceToHost));
4297:     }
4298:     PetscCall(PetscLogGpuToCpu((Ccsr->column_indices->size() + Ccsr->row_offsets->size()) * sizeof(PetscInt)));
4299:     PetscCall(PetscMalloc1(m, &c->ilen));
4300:     PetscCall(PetscMalloc1(m, &c->imax));
4301:     c->maxnz         = c->nz;
4302:     c->nonzerorowcnt = 0;
4303:     c->rmax          = 0;
4304:     for (i = 0; i < m; i++) {
4305:       const PetscInt nn = c->i[i + 1] - c->i[i];
4306:       c->ilen[i] = c->imax[i] = nn;
4307:       c->nonzerorowcnt += (PetscInt) !!nn;
4308:       c->rmax = PetscMax(c->rmax, nn);
4309:     }
4310:     PetscCall(MatMarkDiagonal_SeqAIJ(*C));
4311:     PetscCall(PetscMalloc1(c->nz, &c->a));
4312:     (*C)->nonzerostate++;
4313:     PetscCall(PetscLayoutSetUp((*C)->rmap));
4314:     PetscCall(PetscLayoutSetUp((*C)->cmap));
4315:     Ccusp->nonzerostate = (*C)->nonzerostate;
4316:     (*C)->preallocated  = PETSC_TRUE;
4317:   } else {
4318:     PetscCheck((*C)->rmap->n == B->rmap->n, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_ARG_SIZ, "Invalid number or rows %" PetscInt_FMT " != %" PetscInt_FMT, (*C)->rmap->n, B->rmap->n);
4319:     c = (Mat_SeqAIJ *)(*C)->data;
4320:     if (c->nz) {
4321:       Ccusp = (Mat_SeqAIJHIPSPARSE *)(*C)->spptr;
4322:       PetscCheck(Ccusp->coords, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "Missing coords");
4323:       PetscCheck(Ccusp->format != MAT_HIPSPARSE_ELL && Ccusp->format != MAT_HIPSPARSE_HYB, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_SUP, "Not implemented");
4324:       PetscCheck(Ccusp->nonzerostate == (*C)->nonzerostate, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "Wrong nonzerostate");
4325:       PetscCall(MatSeqAIJHIPSPARSECopyToGPU(A));
4326:       PetscCall(MatSeqAIJHIPSPARSECopyToGPU(B));
4327:       PetscCheck(Acusp->mat, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "Missing Mat_SeqAIJHIPSPARSEMultStruct");
4328:       PetscCheck(Bcusp->mat, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "Missing Mat_SeqAIJHIPSPARSEMultStruct");
4329:       Acsr = (CsrMatrix *)Acusp->mat->mat;
4330:       Bcsr = (CsrMatrix *)Bcusp->mat->mat;
4331:       Ccsr = (CsrMatrix *)Ccusp->mat->mat;
4332:       PetscCheck(Acsr->num_entries == (PetscInt)Acsr->values->size(), PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "A nnz %" PetscInt_FMT " != %" PetscInt_FMT, Acsr->num_entries, (PetscInt)Acsr->values->size());
4333:       PetscCheck(Bcsr->num_entries == (PetscInt)Bcsr->values->size(), PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "B nnz %" PetscInt_FMT " != %" PetscInt_FMT, Bcsr->num_entries, (PetscInt)Bcsr->values->size());
4334:       PetscCheck(Ccsr->num_entries == (PetscInt)Ccsr->values->size(), PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "C nnz %" PetscInt_FMT " != %" PetscInt_FMT, Ccsr->num_entries, (PetscInt)Ccsr->values->size());
4335:       PetscCheck(Ccsr->num_entries == Acsr->num_entries + Bcsr->num_entries, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "C nnz %" PetscInt_FMT " != %" PetscInt_FMT " + %" PetscInt_FMT, Ccsr->num_entries, Acsr->num_entries, Bcsr->num_entries);
4336:       PetscCheck(Ccusp->coords->size() == Ccsr->values->size(), PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "permSize %" PetscInt_FMT " != %" PetscInt_FMT, (PetscInt)Ccusp->coords->size(), (PetscInt)Ccsr->values->size());
4337:       auto pmid = Ccusp->coords->begin();
4338:       thrust::advance(pmid, Acsr->num_entries);
4339:       PetscCall(PetscLogGpuTimeBegin());
4340:       auto zibait = thrust::make_zip_iterator(thrust::make_tuple(Acsr->values->begin(), thrust::make_permutation_iterator(Ccsr->values->begin(), Ccusp->coords->begin())));
4341:       auto zieait = thrust::make_zip_iterator(thrust::make_tuple(Acsr->values->end(), thrust::make_permutation_iterator(Ccsr->values->begin(), pmid)));
4342:       thrust::for_each(zibait, zieait, VecHIPEquals());
4343:       auto zibbit = thrust::make_zip_iterator(thrust::make_tuple(Bcsr->values->begin(), thrust::make_permutation_iterator(Ccsr->values->begin(), pmid)));
4344:       auto ziebit = thrust::make_zip_iterator(thrust::make_tuple(Bcsr->values->end(), thrust::make_permutation_iterator(Ccsr->values->begin(), Ccusp->coords->end())));
4345:       thrust::for_each(zibbit, ziebit, VecHIPEquals());
4346:       PetscCall(MatSeqAIJHIPSPARSEInvalidateTranspose(*C, PETSC_FALSE));
4347:       if (A->form_explicit_transpose && B->form_explicit_transpose && (*C)->form_explicit_transpose) {
4348:         PetscCheck(Ccusp->matTranspose, PETSC_COMM_SELF, PETSC_ERR_COR, "Missing transpose Mat_SeqAIJHIPSPARSEMultStruct");
4349:         PetscBool  AT = Acusp->matTranspose ? PETSC_TRUE : PETSC_FALSE, BT = Bcusp->matTranspose ? PETSC_TRUE : PETSC_FALSE;
4350:         CsrMatrix *AcsrT = AT ? (CsrMatrix *)Acusp->matTranspose->mat : NULL;
4351:         CsrMatrix *BcsrT = BT ? (CsrMatrix *)Bcusp->matTranspose->mat : NULL;
4352:         CsrMatrix *CcsrT = (CsrMatrix *)Ccusp->matTranspose->mat;
4353:         auto       vT    = CcsrT->values->begin();
4354:         if (AT) vT = thrust::copy(AcsrT->values->begin(), AcsrT->values->end(), vT);
4355:         if (BT) thrust::copy(BcsrT->values->begin(), BcsrT->values->end(), vT);
4356:         (*C)->transupdated = PETSC_TRUE;
4357:       }
4358:       PetscCall(PetscLogGpuTimeEnd());
4359:     }
4360:   }
4361:   PetscCall(PetscObjectStateIncrease((PetscObject)*C));
4362:   (*C)->assembled     = PETSC_TRUE;
4363:   (*C)->was_assembled = PETSC_FALSE;
4364:   (*C)->offloadmask   = PETSC_OFFLOAD_GPU;
4365:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
4366: }

4368: static PetscErrorCode MatSeqAIJCopySubArray_SeqAIJHIPSPARSE(Mat A, PetscInt n, const PetscInt idx[], PetscScalar v[])
4369: {
4370:   bool               dmem;
4371:   const PetscScalar *av;

4373:   PetscFunctionBegin;
4374:   dmem = isHipMem(v);
4375:   PetscCall(MatSeqAIJHIPSPARSEGetArrayRead(A, &av));
4376:   if (n && idx) {
4377:     THRUSTINTARRAY widx(n);
4378:     widx.assign(idx, idx + n);
4379:     PetscCall(PetscLogCpuToGpu(n * sizeof(PetscInt)));

4381:     THRUSTARRAY                    *w = NULL;
4382:     thrust::device_ptr<PetscScalar> dv;
4383:     if (dmem) dv = thrust::device_pointer_cast(v);
4384:     else {
4385:       w  = new THRUSTARRAY(n);
4386:       dv = w->data();
4387:     }
4388:     thrust::device_ptr<const PetscScalar> dav = thrust::device_pointer_cast(av);

4390:     auto zibit = thrust::make_zip_iterator(thrust::make_tuple(thrust::make_permutation_iterator(dav, widx.begin()), dv));
4391:     auto zieit = thrust::make_zip_iterator(thrust::make_tuple(thrust::make_permutation_iterator(dav, widx.end()), dv + n));
4392:     thrust::for_each(zibit, zieit, VecHIPEquals());
4393:     if (w) PetscCallHIP(hipMemcpy(v, w->data().get(), n * sizeof(PetscScalar), hipMemcpyDeviceToHost));
4394:     delete w;
4395:   } else PetscCallHIP(hipMemcpy(v, av, n * sizeof(PetscScalar), dmem ? hipMemcpyDeviceToDevice : hipMemcpyDeviceToHost));

4397:   if (!dmem) PetscCall(PetscLogCpuToGpu(n * sizeof(PetscScalar)));
4398:   PetscCall(MatSeqAIJHIPSPARSERestoreArrayRead(A, &av));
4399:   PetscFunctionReturn(PETSC_SUCCESS);
4400: }
